### Mark for Death Reverse Strategies ###

X01_mark_for_death = {
    allowed = {
		original_tag = X01
	}
    enable = {
		has_country_flag = OG_mark_for_death_flag_X01
    }
    enable_reverse = {
		is_subject = no
		any_other_country = {
			has_country_flag = OG_mark_for_death_flag_X01
		}
    }
    reversed = yes
    abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {
		type = conquer
		id = X01
		value = 100
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = declare_war
		id = X01
		value = 100
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = X01
		value = 50
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = diplo_action_desire

		original_tag = Y09
	}
    enable = {
		has_country_flag = OG_mark_for_death_flag_Y09
    }
    enable_reverse = {
		is_subject = no
		any_other_country = {
			has_country_flag = OG_mark_for_death_flag_Y09
		}
    }
    reversed = yes
    abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {
		type = conquer
		id = Y09
		value = 100
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = declare_war
		id = Y09
		value = 100
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = Y09
		value = 50
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = diplo_action_desire
		id = Y09
		target = generate_wargoal
		value = 100
	}
}

    }
    enable_reverse = {
		is_subject = no
		any_other_country = {
			has_country_flag = OG_mark_for_death_flag_Z16
		}
    }
    reversed = yes
    abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {
		type = conquer
		id = Z16
		value = 100
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = declare_war
		id = Z16
		value = 100
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = Z16
		value = 50
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = diplo_action_desire
		id = Z16
		target = generate_wargoal
		value = 100
	}
}

### These reverse strategies make landlocked AI always want to have some kind of access to the sea when at war alongside somebody else -> good for sending troops to non-neighbouring allies. ###

X01_military_access_sea_route = {
    allowed = {
		original_tag = X01
	}
    enable = {
		is_neighbor_of = X01
		NOT = {
			is_ally_with = X01						# Would be redundant.
			has_war_with = X01
		}
		any_controlled_state = {
			is_coastal = yes
		}
    }
    enable_reverse = {
		has_war = yes
		any_other_country = {
			has_war_together_with = X01				# Strat is useless if we're alone.
		}
		capital_sea_access_scripted_trigger = no	# Strat is useless if we already have sea access.
    }
    reversed = yes
    abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {									# LET ME THROOOUUUGH!
		type = diplo_action_desire
		id = X01
		target = military_access
		value = 100
	}
}

    allowed = {
       original_tag = Y84
    }
    enable = {
		is_neighbor_of = Y84
		NOT = {
			is_ally_with = Y84
			has_war_with = Y84
		}
		any_controlled_state = {
			is_coastal = yes
		}
    }
    enable_reverse = {
		has_war = yes
		any_other_country = {
			has_war_together_with = Y84
		}
		capital_sea_access_scripted_trigger = no
    }
    reversed = yes
    abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {
		type = diplo_action_desire
		id = Y84
		target = military_access
		value = 100
	}

			has_war_together_with = Z16
		}
		capital_sea_access_scripted_trigger = no
    }
    reversed = yes
    abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = {
		type = diplo_action_desire
		id = Z16
		target = military_access
		value = 100
	}
}

	}
}
